msg:The carefully selected hotel did not disappoint me. I feel that their hotel has the best night view among hotels in the same price range. Although it is not close to Hongya Cave, I can see Hongya Cave and Qiansimen Bridge at the same time. The hotel's service is also very good. If you call the front desk and ask for something, it will be delivered quickly. There are also robots to help deliver takeaways to your door. The cleaning lady will help fold clothes. The minibar is replenished every day, and Coke, Sprite, and Fanta are all available. One bottle, after discovering that I love drinking water, I was provided with four bottles of Nongfu Spring every day. The hotel has an excellent location and is very convenient to go anywhere. I experienced the hotel breakfast for a day, which included noodles, porridge, fruits, soy milk, juice, bacon sausage, bread, etc. It was quite rich and not expensive. The only thing that needs attention is the design of the bathtub in the room. If the water outlet volume is turned to the maximum, there will be splashing, which may easily cause the floor to be slippery. Just reduce the water volume. All in all, it was a very pleasant experience. I will choose this hotel next time I come to Chongqing.
